import 'package:supabase_flutter/supabase_flutter.dart';

Future listenToOrderStatus(int orderID) async {
// Add your function code here!
final client = Supabase.instance.client;
StreamSubscription<List<Map<String, dynamic>>>? _streamSubscription = null;
_streamSubscription = client
.from('orders')
.stream(primaryKey: ['id'])
.eq('id', orderID)
.listen((List<Map<String, dynamic>> data) {
for (final order in data) {
final status = order['status'];
if (status == 'issued') {
FFAppState().orderIsIssued = true;
_streamSubscription!.cancel();
} else if (status == 'cancel') {
// Additional action for 'cancel' status
_streamSubscription!.cancel(); // Close the stream
}
}
});
